Item: 
Gift of Ferocity
Binds when picked up
Unique
Use:
Permanently adds the effect of when shapeshifting into Cat form the Druid gains 20 energy, when shapeshifting into Bear form the Druid gains 5 rage to a head slot item. Does not stack with other enchantments for the selected equipment slot.
"Blessed by Cenarius, this gift beholds the sheer ferocity of nature itself."
